KHRIMS GNYIS THOB STE, DE YANG BDEN PA DANG PO GNYIS KYI DON

RTOGS PA NA BDEN PA'I DON LA YID CHES

PA'I DAD PA 'BYUNG BAS CHOS LA SHES NAS DAD PA THOB PA YIN LA,
DE DANG DUS MNYAM DU ZAG MED KYI SPONG BA BDUN YANG THOB PAS

DGYES PA'I TSUL KHRIMS NI ZAG MED KYI SDOM PA NYID LAS GZHAN
DU MED PA'I PHYIR RO, ,LAM BDEN

BDEN RNAMS SANGS RGYAS DANG DGE 'DUN DU BYED PA'I CHOS YIN PAS
NA, SANGS RGYAS DANG DE'I NYAN THOS KYI DGE 'DUN LA YANG SHES
NAS DAD PA THOB PA

YIN NO, ,DES NA BDEN PA DANG PO GSUM MNGON SUM DU RTOGS MA

LAM BDEN MNGON SUM DU RTOGS PA NAS SHES NAS DAD PA BZHI CHAR
THOB PA YIN NO, ,SKABS

LA, RANG GI NGOS SKAL GYI 'DOD CHAGS DANG BRAL BYED NI MA YIN
TE, SBYOR BA'I LAM SOGS GSUM NI SPONG LAM BAR CHAD MED LAM MA
YIN PA'I PHYIR DANG, PHYI MA GNYIS PAR

CHAD MED LAM YIN KYANG RANG GI NGOS SKAL GYI 'DOD NYON MTHONG
LAM GYI SNGA ROL NAS SPANGS ZIN PA'I PHYIR, RANG GI SPANG
BYA'I 'DOD CHAGS DANG BRAL BYED YIN LA YID 'BYUNG BYED MA YIN
PA NI, CHAGS BRAL SNGON SONG GI PHYIR MI 'ONG ZHUGS PA'I 'GOG
LAM CHOS BZOD GNYIS LAS GZHAN PA'I 'GOG LAM LA

DMIGS NAS RANG GI SPANG BYA DNGOS SU SPONG BYED KYI BAR CHAD
MED LAM THAMS CAD DE, DE DAG RANG RANG GI SPANG BYA'I 'DOD
CHAGS DANG 'BREL BYED NI YIN LA, YID 'BYUNG BYED NI MA YIN TE,
YUL 'GOG LAM GNYIS MCHOG TU DGA' BA'I GNAS YIN PA LAS SKYO
BA'I GNAS MA YIN PA'I PHYIR, CHAGS BRAL SNGON

SONG GI PHYIR MI 'ONG ZHUGS PA'I 'GOG LAM CHOS BZOD GNYIS NI
RANG GI SPANG BYA'I 'DOD CHAGS DANG BRAL BYED MA YIN PA SNGA
MA DANG MTSUNGS SO, ,GNYIS KA YIN PA NI, CHAGS BRAL SNGON SONG
GI PHYIR MI 'ONG ZHUGS PA'I RGYUD KYI SDUG KUN CHOS BZOD GNYIS
LAS GZHAN PA'I SDUG KUN LA DMIGS PA'I RJES

@56B BZOD SOGS BDEN PA DE GNYIS LA DMIGS PA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM
THAMS CAD DE, YID 'BYUNG BA'I DNGOS PO LA DMIGS PA'I PHYIR
DANG, RANG GI NGOS SKAL GYI NYON MONGS DNGOS SU SPONG BYED YIN
PA'I PHYIR, GNYIS KA MA YIN PA NI 'GOG LAM LA DMIGS PA'I SBYOR
BA DANG, RNAM GROL DANG, KHYAD

PAR CAN GYI LAM RNAMS DANG, CHAGS BRAL SNGON SONG GI PHYIR MI
'ONG ZHUGS PA'I RGYUD KYI 'GOG LAM CHOS BZOD LA SOGS PA STE,
RGYU MTSAN GONG DU BKOD PA RNAMS KYIS SHES SO, ,'DI DAG GI TSE
YANG YID 'BYUNG BYED DANG, RANG GI SPANG BYA'I 'DOD CHAGS DANG
BRAL BYED ZHES SOGS TSIG SKYON MA BCAD NA RTZOD PA'I TSE

KHAS LEN 'DZIN DKA' BAR 'ONG NGO, ,DE LA KHO NA RE, 'GOG LAM
GNYIS YID 'BYUNG BYA YIN PAR THAL, LAM BDEN YID 'BYUNG BYA YIN
PA'I PHYIR, DER THAL, YID NGES PAR 'BYUNG BYA YIN PA'I PHYIR
TE, NGES PAR 'BYUNG BYA YIN PA'I PHYIR ZER NA MA KHYAB, DER
THAL, DE DAG NYID DUS GTAM GZHI DANG, ,NGES PAR 'BYUNG

BCAS GZHI DANG BCAS, ,ZHES PA'I 'GREL PAR, LAM BDEN KYANG NGES
PAR 'BYUNG BYA YIN TE, LHAG MED KYI TSE DOR BAR BYA BA YIN
PA'I PHYIR, ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, TSOGS SBYOR MTHONG SGOM MI
SLOB LAM RNAMS DANG, ,ZHUGS DANG GNAS PA'I KHYAD PAR LA SOGS
PA'I, ,TSIG DON MTHA' DPYOD GSAL BAR BKOD

PA 'DI, ,BLO GSAL THAR 'DOD 'JUG PA'I LAM DU SPEL, ,CHOS MNGON
PA MDZOD KYI DGONGS DON GSAL BAR BYED PA LEGS BSHAD NYIN BYED
DBANG PO'I SNANG BA LAS, LAM DANG GANG ZAG BSTAN PA ZHES BYA
BA GNAS DRUG PA'I RNAM PAR BSHAD PA'O,, ,,
